msg:3 days stays.

The hotel decoration and color palette is very good. The room was well made, water flow and hot water is consistent in the shower room. You have some selection of movies/programmes to watch for free, TV is very responsive, there are some useful mechanisms like motorized curtains and a smart toilet 

Next to the hotel you can find a very convenient mall to have some food and drinks: pizza hut, changee, heytea, dairy queen, mcdonald, starbucks, etc. There is also a walmart. But apart from this mall there is nothing much nearby, no local street food around the area.

Service overall is good, you will have some difficulties to communicate in English as most of the staff doesn‚Äôt speak it.

Although the gym room is big and spacious, I would have expected more equipments.

What let me down the most was the food (breakfast buffet) specifically the pastries and bread are not good nor fresh, those are most likely from day(s) before. Among all the food stations, the noodles one is the best. Apart from this, there is nothing special for foodies.

For the price, I would have expected more

I feel that because Xiamen's tourism has cooled down, there have been no new hotels in recent years, and the five-star hotels I stayed in before are also quite old (although the transportation on the island is relatively convenient, the Xiamen subway is actually very convenient, and it only takes 30 minutes to take a taxi to anywhere).
This Indigo is really good, with a Western design sense + fusion style, a very reasonable layout of room dynamics, the bedding is as high as ever, and the window of the bathtub gives people a little surprise (discover it yourself~).
Fiona, the customer relations director at the front desk, and Victoria, the check-in lady, are very nice. They keep asking if there is anything they can help with, and they will remember your name until you check out.
I think the Shacha noodles for breakfast are better than those eaten outside~
The concierge will help open the car door and carry the luggage every time~

In short, in a service-oriented city in the south, I give this Indigo a full score!
